The Council will review national policy for science, technology and innovation to develop a new generation of scientists #WorldGovSummit
The UAE Council of Scientists will be established as an advisory body, and will include leading researchers and academics #WorldGovSummit
The post of Minister of State for Tolerance has been created to promote tolerance as a fundamental value in UAE society #WorldGovSummit
The Ministry of Cabinet Affairs, tasked with future strategies, becomes the Ministry of Cabinet Affairs and The Future. #WorldGovSummit
The Ministry of Development and International Cooperation will merge with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs #WorldGovSummit
We merged the National Tourism Council and the Ministry of the Economy, and developed national GDP targets for the sector #WorldGovSummit
Managing climate change makes the Ministry of Environment and Water, into the Ministry of Climate Change and Environment #WorldGovSummit
A new post, Minister of State for Happiness, will align and drive government policy to create social good and satisfaction. #WorldGovSummit
Focusing on Emirati family and society, the Ministry of Social Affairs will become the Ministry for Community Development. #WorldGovSummit
The Marriage Fund will be merged into the Ministry of Social Affairs. Nurseries will fall under the Ministry of Education. #WorldGovSummit
We are also reforming the Ministry of Labour to better manage the UAE workforce in this new era of development. #WorldGovSummit
An independent entity will oversee public hospitals in the UAE: a structural change to the Ministry of Health's portfolio. #WorldGovSummit
We have established the Higher Education and Human Resources Council to restructure the development of our human resources #WorldGovSummit
We are creating the Emirates Schools Establishment to manage public schools as an autonomous, semi-independent authority. #WorldGovSummit
The changes include merging the Ministries of Education and Higher Education, with two state ministers in support. #WorldGovSummit
The new government will have less Ministries, with more Ministers able to manage changing and dynamic strategic portfolios #WorldGovSummit
The President of the UAE has approved the largest structural change in the history of our federal government. #WorldGovSummit

Regional Challenges demand clear Arab economic vision, big economic projects & effective utilization of human & natural resources
Future of Arab World depends on great developmental & economic revival, led by GCC, achieved in cooperation with our brothers and friends.
Decrease in oil prices had positive impact on growth of many economic sectors, and state of region established unique economic model for UAE
Financial sector saw double-digit growth in 2014 of some 15%, with contributions to gross domestic product reaching AED 122B
20 million tourists visiting the seven emirates in 2014, as we are working on infrastructure projects to double these numbers
National production reached AED 2.5T in 2014, with AED 450B in manufacturing industries, AED 295B in construction sector
Total compensation paid to employees in 2014 AED 410B, incl. AED 82 billion in government sector
Our exports (inclusive of re-exports) reached AED 376B, we continue to lead Middle East as global economies’ largest trading partner
Our imports reached some AED 700B, non-oil sectors contributed 68.6% of GDP, goal is 80% by 2021
2014 strongest year for UAE’s economy, GDP grew by 4.6% reaching AED 1.47T, non-oil sectors grew by 8.1%
Today I have published a note on the state of UAE’s economy covering also an important directions for the period to come
التحديات التي تمر بها منطقتنا بحاجة لتنفيذ رؤية عربية واضحة وإطلاق مشاريع اقتصادية ضخمة ،واستغلال الموارد البشرية والطبيعية بشكل أكثر فعالية
مستقبل منطقتنا العربية مرهون بتحقيق نهضة تنموية واقتصادية كبرى تقودها دول الخليج مجتمعة بالتعاون مع الأشقاء والأصدقاء
احب أن أستغل هذه الفرصة أيها الإخوة للدعوة لأخذ خطوات جدية لتحقيق تكامل اقتصادي خليجي لضمان استقرار المنطقة العربية كلها
انخفاض أسعار النفط حفز النمو الإيجابي في قطاعات أخرى، والظروف المحيطة بالمنطقة رسخت نموذجا اقتصاديا فريدا لدولة الإمارات
لدينا نمو في قطاع المشاريع المالية بنسبة 15% في عام 2014 ، و122 مليار درهم حجم مساهمته في الناتج المحلي الإجمالي للدولة
20 مليون سائح لكافة إمارات الدولة في 2014 ، ونعمل على مشاريع بنى تحتية ومرافق ترفيهية بعشرات المليارات لمضاعفة الأعداد
في ٢٠١٤ بلغت القيمة الإجمالية للإنتاج 2.5 تريليون درهم ، والانتاج في القطاع الصناعي 450 مليار ، وفي التشييد والبناء 295 مليار درهم
بلغ إجمالي الأجور في قطاعاتنا الاقتصادية 410 مليار درهم في 2014 ، منها 82 مليار في القطاع الحكومي ،والإمارات الأولى عربيا في اقتصاد المعرفة
كما بلغ إجمالي صادراتنا شاملة إعادة التصدير 376 مليار درهم في 2014 ،والإمارات تتصدر دول الشرق الاوسط كأكبر شريك لأهم الاقتصادات العالمية
لامست وارداتنا 700 مليار درهم في 2014 ، ومساهمة القطاعات الغير نفطية في الاقتصاد الوطني تصل 68.6% وهدفنا الوصول لنسبة 80% في عام 2021
عام 2014 هو العام الأقوى اقتصاديا، الناتج الإجمالي بلغ 1.47 تريليون درهم، والقطاعات غير النفطية حققت نموا 8.1 % والناتج المحلي الإجمالي 4.6%
الإخوة والأخوات نشرت اليوم رسالة تتعلق بحالة اقتصاد الدولة وأهم توجهاته المستقبلية، تعزيزا للشفافية وإطلاقا لعادة سنوية ،وهذه بعض مقتطفاتها

UAE Reserve forces will consist of retired armed forces’ soldiers and national service program graduates.
The Service will cover military training at the armed forces, 9 months for high school grads & 2 yrs for those with less than high school.
The National Service will be mandatory for all male UAE nationals, above 18 yrs, or high school grads; it will be voluntary for females.
The new law adds another layer to the national defense force to further protect our nation, secure its borders & preserve its achievements.
